    e_F(nu) (Jy) (F8.5)  ? rms uncertainty on F(nu)dnu [ucd=ERROR]
    n_F(nu)      (A1)    [:] : For Bl 2-1, E{nu}=K.011, modified in 0.011 [ucd=NOTE]
    r_F(nu)      (a14)   References for nu data, in refs.dat file [ucd=REFER_CODE]
    F(5) (Jy)    (F6.3)  ? Flux density at 5GHz (G2) [ucd=PHOT_FLUX_RADIO_5G]
    cr           (F5.2)  ? Radio extinction constant (G2) (1) [ucd=PHOT_EXTINCTION_ISM]
    n_cr         (A1)    [E] E: Err, no data [ucd=NOTE]
    calpha       (F6.3)  ? Optical extinction constant (G2) (2) [ucd=PHOT_EXTINCTION_ISM]
    e_calpha     (F5.2)  ? rms uncertainty on calpha [ucd=ERROR]
    r_calpha     (a50)   References for alpha data, in refs.dat file [ucd=REFER_CODE]
